<div id="review_1152183784" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1152183784" />
    <a title="Barbara H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1883816-barbara-h"><img alt="Barbara H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572546566p2/1883816.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1152183784?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Barbara H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Barbara H" href="/user/show/1883816-barbara-h">Barbara H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1152183784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6392259276044617359"> Hoffman has bestowed the name Story on this family to illustrate that this is a many-storied novel about storytellers, replete with enchantment and sorrow, atonement and faithfulness. The young Story sisters, three dark-haired beauties, live a charmed and loving existence, spinning fairy tales and sharing a private language. This all-female household, (compared as a sly variation on Little Women), is under a grim spell, and not even loving visits with their fairy-godmother-like grandmother in P</span>
  <span id="freeText6392259276044617359" style="display:none"> Hoffman has bestowed the name Story on this family to illustrate that this is a many-storied novel about storytellers, replete with enchantment and sorrow, atonement and faithfulness. The young Story sisters, three dark-haired beauties, live a charmed and loving existence, spinning fairy tales and sharing a private language. This all-female household, (compared as a sly variation on Little Women), is under a grim spell, and not even loving visits with their fairy-godmother-like grandmother in Paris offers relief. As the girls grow older and enter their teen years the whole atmosphere develops subtle and marked transformations. The expected, triad of "sex, drugs and rock and roll" become difficult factors, with wide ranging effects. I will not interject spoilers here, but will allow others to experience this novel with a fresh perspective.<br /><br />As frequently seen in Hoffman's novels, nature's powerful presence reflects in human behavior, and consequently, the Story girls attach much significance to storms, ghosts, and plant and animal spirits. Her portrayal of Nature and the world around these girls is vivid and almost tangible. The characters are soulful, with palpable suffering and many sorrows . Despite my description here I would not classify this book as a fantasy. Of interest to me in reading this was the fact that I was unsure whether to continue initially, but Hoffman's narrative became richer and more enticing as I continued.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6392259276044617359" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Tressa " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/226335-tressa"><img alt="Tressa " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464796958p2/226335.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/60201724?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tressa " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tressa " href="/user/show/226335-tressa">Tressa </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/226335-tressa?shelf=general-fiction">general-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer60201724" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12217544846348094016">I have officially just stayed up all night long to finish the remaining 3/4 of The Story Sisters, something I have done infrequently in my life. I have to get up and go to work in another two hours, but I won't be able to sleep, so what do I care?<br/><br/>Like another favorite female author of mine--Anne Tyler--Alice Hoffman knows how to spin a story about the mundane parts of our lives, but also the magical moments. Characters are introduced on a whim or chance meeting, and they may serve as an anchor i</span>
  <span id="freeText12217544846348094016" style="display:none">I have officially just stayed up all night long to finish the remaining 3/4 of The Story Sisters, something I have done infrequently in my life. I have to get up and go to work in another two hours, but I won't be able to sleep, so what do I care?<br /><br />Like another favorite female author of mine--Anne Tyler--Alice Hoffman knows how to spin a story about the mundane parts of our lives, but also the magical moments. Characters are introduced on a whim or chance meeting, and they may serve as an anchor in another character's life, or they my never be heard from again. Just like in the real world.<br /><br />This story takes place in America and Paris, and it tells the story of three sisters who were so close in childhood, they created a make-believe world called Arnelle and spoke its secret language until tragedy and/or puberty planted them firmly in this world.<br /><br />The Story Sisters is about what families do for one another and to one another because of love and hate and jealousy and forgiveness. A stunning story and one I'd recommend to anyone.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12217544846348094016" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('G2Sygw0ELCuqZN8cH4jFDwcfrsw0U0gwrUdLfzJ6P1DaaLTmb9Vl1FPxfzhrgDaV9+05/CNBPk8rxS/QvxqoCQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZvYAJK5T4cZK3qJ9s7kHjL1c+Qpk+jWImLdn8xdig2mn+gZBzIKoObNLAlnHsfQWTa5uOnPoQ/ceNQNcmgIUMA==')})
  }

Ana’s impetuous streak occasionally invites danger. Armed only with the contents of her purse, and with the help of new chums Midge, Velma, and a dashing female police officer named Jackie, the plucky but innocent Cherry must save her aunt, find a gaggle of missing nuns, and stop an illegal land grab — all under the warm gaze of her hero, girl detective Nancy Clue. And when the queer caper has ended, will there be a chance for Nancy and Cherry?Mabel Maney’s camp classic The Case of the Not-So-Nice Nurse has been beloved by readers since it was first published in 1993. This sparkling parody of 1950s girl adventure stories will make you laugh out loud and long for a lemon Jell-O mold.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/3502.Alice_Hoffman">About Alice Hoffman</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/3502.Alice_Hoffman"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1590599928p3/3502.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/3502.Alice_Hoffman">Alice Hoffman

<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>

followers

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17198340072578885199">Alice Hoffman is the author of more than thirty works of fiction, including The World That We Knew, The Rules of Magic, The Marriage of Opposites, Practical Magic, The Red Garden, the Oprah’s Book Club selection Here on Earth, The Museum of Extraordinary Things, and The Dovekeepers. Her most recent novel is The World That We Knew. She lives near Boston.</span>

</div>
